This means:\n\n1. If a timeout occurs before the first suspend, the controller is in degraded mode\n2. These flags are never reset during suspend/resume. During resume, azx_resume/azx_runtime_resume call azx_init_chip(chip, 1), but azx_init_chip skips CORB/RIRB reinitialization when chip->single_cmd is 1 (line 1222-1223: 'if (!chip->single_cmd) azx_init_cmd_io(chip)'). Additionally, azx_reset only enables unsolicited responses if chip->single_cmd is 0 (lines 1105-1107). As a result, the controller remains in degraded single-command mode after resume, causing codec communication failures, timeouts, and choppy audio output.
